<p><a href = vnd.unilang:abbreviation.html>Abbreviation</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">geneva</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> alternatively <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">genever</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:juniper.html>juniper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">genevre</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">genièvre</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iūniperus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:juniper.html>juniper</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:hence.html>Hence</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gin.html>gin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rummy.html>rummy</a></i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>first</a> attested 1941).

</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn
